 The Story of My Life with Bhagwan Rajneesh 'describes her experiences, observations and feelings of her time when she was working with Osho Rajneesh

 ‚Äô As lifestyles have changed over time, technology has become our need
 ek samay tha jabacamerakisi uplakshya yaa aayojan ke dauraan hi kaam aata tha, lekin aisa lagata he jaise ab is takanic ne hamaare dainik jivan main apni ek khaas jagah bana lee he
 As such, today it is common to have a digital camera in every smartphone or a great feature phone
 lekin samay ke saath photography yaa yah kahen ki jindagi ke palon ko tasveeron main sanjone kii hasarat badi he
 Digital camera sales have also increased a lot these days in non-phone gadgets stores
 lekin aise main sabase jaruri yah jaan lenaa he ki koun sa camera liya jaae or camera kharidte vakt kin baton kaa khyal rakhaa jaae
 1) Ask yourself these eight questions - Why do you need a camera? - What kind of photography do you want to do with the camera? (portraits, landscape or sports) - Under what circumstances would you do photography? (indoor, outdoor, low light, bright light) - Do you do photography in auto mode or would like to learn the art of photography? - How much do you know about the camera, do you like to do manual photography? Looking for different features? (zoom, image stabilization, fancy or large screen) - How important is the size and weight of the camera to you? - What is your budget? These questions determine to a great extent what your camera should be
 aam taur par showrooms main celsman bhi aapse yahi sawaal karata he
 It is quite possible that he can use your answers to his advantage and give you the product that you do not really need
 2) megapixl ke moh ko tyaag denaam taur par camere ko bechate vakt jis ek cheez kii sabase adhik charchaa hoti he, vah he megapixl
 These days most digital cameras come with at least 5 megapixels
 camera kitne megapixl kaa ho yah aapaki jarurat par nirbhar karata he
 Before making any decision towards this, decide whether you will print the pictures taken? If yes, what will be its size
 kyonki saamaanya sies main printing ke liye 4 yaa usase adhik megapixl kaa camera paryaapt he
 Think of it in such a way that the megapixel directly determines how big your picture can be without being pixelated
 jabaki jarurat se adhik megapixl se ek ghaataa yah he ki megapixl badhane ke saath hi har tasviir aapke memory card main zyada spes legi
 3) Accessories: What you will get along with buying the camera, along with its features, also check what is going to be found in the extras
 jo chijen aapke liye jaruri hai, unamem- camera cese, memory card, atirikt betry, charger, lens (agar DSLR camera he to), filter, trypod, monopod, ekstranal flash, riflector aadi
 Actually, these are the things that you need in the end
 isliye behatar deal tay karen
 4) Search for other offers If accessories are less with the camera, then look for other deals
 online or ritel bazaar main bhi is tarah ke kai ophers milte hai
 5) DSLR or Compact Point and Shoot These days DSLR camera has become more of a status symbol
 lekin jaruri nahin ki yah aapke kaam kaa ho
 Think of it in such a way that if you want to do normal photography in auto mode then it is not much useful for you
 saath hi yah zyada vajani or mahangaa he
 Its cleaning and maintenance process is also complex
 lekin agar aap photography kii kala ko siikhnaa chaahate hai
 Manual photography rather than auto mode attracts you then DSLR camera is right for you
 7) optical juum ko chunecamaron main do tarah ke juum aate hai
 One digital and the other optical
 behatar hogaoptical juumavaale camere kaa chunaav karen
 Digital zoom camera only increases the pixels of your shot
 isse aapako subject bada dikhne lagata he
 But this makes the picture pixelated
 dhyaan rakhen ki aapkaa camera kam se kam 3x optical juum vaala ho
 This means that it will make your subject three times larger
 7) rivyuu padhencamera kharidne se pehle thodaa homework kar len
 Choose the model of camera according to your needs and budget
 phir online yaa magazine main chhapane vaale rivyuu ko padhein
 If buying online, read the customer review as well
 8) first hand experionssho room se camera kharid rahe hai to camera haath main lekar achche se jaanch len
 That means whether the camera fits in your hands or not
 aap uske saath confort feel kar rahe hai yaa nahin
 Take a picture or two
 saare opshan or fitures ko jaanch len
 9) Negotiation As a customer, bargaining is your birthright
 apane is adhikaar kaa prayog jarur karen
 Compare prices online and buy only
 ritel bazaar se kharid rahe hai to kai saare store par discount ofer kii jaankaree icttha karne ke baad hi product khariden
